list_of_title = df['Movie_Title'].tolist()
find_close_match= difflib.get_close_matches(name,list_of_title)
close_match = find_close_match[0]
index_movie =df[df.Movie_Title == close_match]['Movie_ID'].values[0]
rec_score = list(enumerate(sim_scr[index_movie]))
sort1 = sorted(rec_score,key = lambda x:x[1],reverse =True)

print("TOP 10 MOVIES FOR YOU : \n")
